<script>
function switchTab(btn, tabId) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.admin-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(c => c.style.display = 'none');
  
  btn.classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById(tabId).style.display = 'block';
}

function adminOpenVariantModal(parentId, productName, brand) {
  const modal = document.getElementById('product-modal');
  const form = document.getElementById('product-form');
  
  form.reset();
  modal.classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('product-modal-title').textContent = `Add Variant for ${productName}`;
  document.getElementById('variant-tab-btn').style.display = 'none'; // Hide variant tab when adding a new variant
  
  switchTab(document.querySelector('.admin-tab'), 'tab-general');
  
  form.querySelector('[name="id"]').value = '';
  form.querySelector('[name="parent_id"]').value = parentId;
  form.querySelector('[name="name"]').value = productName;
  form.querySelector('[name="brand"]').value = brand;
  form.querySelector('[name="code"]').focus();
  
  showToast('Adding new variant. Please enter a unique Product Code.', 'info');
}

function adminOpenVariantModalFromTab() {
  const form = document.getElementById('product-form');
  const parentId = form.querySelector('[name="id"]').value;
  const productName = form.querySelector('[name="name"]').value;
  const brand = form.querySelector('[name="brand"]').value;
  
  adminOpenVariantModal(parentId, productName, brand);
}

// Override modal open to handle tabs and title
document.querySelectorAll('[data-modal="product-modal"]').forEach(btn => {
  btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
    const isEdit = !!btn.dataset.id;
    document.getElementById('product-modal-title').textContent = isEdit ? 'Edit Product' : 'Add New Product';
    document.getElementById('variant-tab-btn').style.display = (isEdit && !btn.dataset.parentId) ? 'block' : 'none';
    switchTab(document.querySelector('.admin-tab'), 'tab-general');
  });
});

async function adminDeleteProduct(productId) {
  if (!confirm('Are you sure you want to PERMANENTLY remove this product? This cannot be undone.')) return;
  
  try {
    const response = await fetch(`/oriflame-admin-panel-x9k2/products/${productId}/delete`, {
      method: 'POST'
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    
    if (data.success) {
      showToast(data.message, 'success');
      setTimeout(() => location.reload(), 1000);
    } else {
      showToast(data.message || 'Failed to remove product', 'error');
    }
  } catch (err) {
    showToast('Something went wrong', 'error');
  }
}

async function adminToggleProductStatus(productId) {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(`/oriflame-admin-panel-x9k2/products/${productId}/toggle-status`, {
      method: 'POST'
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    
    if (data.success) {
      showToast(data.message, 'success');
      setTimeout(() => location.reload(), 1000);
    } else {
      showToast(data.message || 'Failed to toggle status', 'error');
    }
  } catch (err) {
    showToast('Something went wrong', 'error');
  }
}
</script>
